śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhuḥ 
bhagavadbhaktibhedanirūpakaḥ
pūrvavibhāgaḥ 
sāmānyabhaktiḥ
prathamalaharī
śrīśrīrādhāgovindadevau vijayete
akhilarasāmṛtamūrtiḥ prasṛmararuciruddhatārakāpāliḥ 
kalitaśyāmālalito rādhāpreyān vidhur jayati  RBhrs 
hṛdi yasya preraṇayā pravartito 'haṃ varākarūpo 'pi 
tasya hareḥ padakamalaṃ vande caitanyadevasya  RBhrs 
viśrāmamandiratyā tasya sanātanatanor madīśasya 
bhaktirasāmṛtasindhur bhavatu sadāyam pramodāya  RBhrs 
bhaktirasāmṛtasindhau carataḥ paribhūtakālajālabhiyaḥ 
bhaktamakarān aśīlitamuktinadīkān namasāmi  RBhrs 
mīmāṃsakabaḍavāgneḥ kaṭhinām api kuṇṭhayann asau 
sphuratu sanātana suciraṃ tava bhaktirasāmṛtāmbhodhiḥ  RBhrs 
bhaktirasasya prastutir akhilajagaṅmaṅgalaprasaṅgasya 
ajñenāpi mayāsya kriyate suhṛdām pramodāya  RBhrs 
etasya bhagavadbhaktirasāmṛtapayonidheḥ 
catvārah khalu vakṣyante bhāgāḥ pūrvādayaḥ kramāt  RBhrs 
tatra pūrve vibhāge 'smin bhaktibhedanirūpake 
anukrameṇa vaktavyaṃ laharīṇāṃ catuṣṭayam  RBhrs 
ādyā sāmānyabhaktyāḍhyā dvitīyā sādhanānvitā 
bhāvāśritā tṛtīyā ca turyā premanirūpikā  RBhrs 
tatrādau suṣṭhu vaiśiṣṭyam asyāḥ kathayituṃ sphuṭam 
lakṣaṇaṃ kriyate bhakter uttamāyāḥ satāṃ matam  RBhrs 
anyābhilāṣitāśūnyaṃ jñānakarmādyanāvṛtam 
ānukūlyena kṛṣṇānuśīlanaṃ bhaktir uttamā  RBhrs 
yathā śrīnāradapañcarātre
sarvopādhivinirmuktaṃ tatparatvena nirmalam 
hṛṣīkeṇa hṛṣīkeśasevanaṃ bhaktir ucyate  RBhrs 
śrībhāgavatasya tṛtīyaskandhe ca 
ahaituky avyavahitā yā bhaktiḥ puruṣottame  RBhrs 
sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpyasārūpyaikatvam apy uta 
dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  RBhrs 
sa eva bhaktiyogākhya ātyantika udāhṛtaḥ  RBhrs 
sālokyetyādipadyasthabhaktotkarṣaṇirūpaṇam 
bhakter viśuddhatāvyaktyā lakṣaṇe paryavasyati  RBhrs 
kleśaghnī śubhadā mokṣalaghutākṛt sudurlabhā 
sāndrānandaviśeṣātmā śrīkṛṣṇākarṣiṇī ca sā  RBhrs 
tatrāsyāḥ kleśaghnatvam 
kleśās tu pāpaṃ tadbījam avidyā ceti te tridhā  RBhrs 
tatra pāpam
aprārabdhaṃ bhavet pāpaṃ prārabdhaṃ ceti tad dvidhā  RBhrs 
tatra aprārabdhaharatvam
yathā ekaḍaśe 
yathāgniḥ susamiddhārciḥ karoty edhāṃsi bhasmasāt 
tathā madviṣayābhaktir uddhavaināṃsi kṛtsnaśaḥ  RBhrs 
prārabdhaharatvam
yathā tṛtīye 
yannāmadheyaśravaṇānukīrtanād
yatprahvaṇad yatsmaraṇād api kvacit 
śvādo 'pi sadyaḥ savanāya kalpate
kutaḥ punas te bhagavan nu darśanāt  RBhrs 
durjātir eva savanāyogyatve kāraṇam matam 
durjātyārambhakaṃ pāpaṃ yat syāt prārabdham eva tat  RBhrs 
padmapurāne ca
aprārabdhaphalaṃ pāpaṃ kūṭaṃ bījaṃ phalonmukham 
krameṇaiva pralīyeta viṣṇubhaktiratātmanām  RBhrs 
bījaharatvam
yathā ṣaṣṭhe 
tais tāny aghāni pūyante tapodānavratādibhiḥ 
nādharmajaṃ tadhṛdayaṃ tad apīśāṅghrisevayā  RBhrs 
avidyāharatvam
yathā caturthe 
yatpādapaṅkajapalāśavilāsabhaktyā
karmāśayaṃ grathitam udgrathayanti santaḥ 
tadvan na riktamatayo yatayo 'pi ruddha
srotogaṇās tam araṇaṃ bhaja vāsudevam  RBhrs 
pādme ca
kṛtānuyātrāvidyābhir haribhaktir anuttamā 
avidyāṃ nirdahaty āśu dāvajvāleva pannagīm  RBhrs 
śubhadatvam
śubhāni prīṇanaṃ sarvajagatām anuraktatā 
sadguṇāḥ sukham ityādīny ākhyātāni manīṣibhiḥ  RBhrs 
tatra jagatprīṇanādidvayapradatvam
yathā pādme
yenārcito haris tena tarpitāni jaganty api 
rajyanti jantavas tatra jangamāḥ sthāvarā api  RBhrs 
sadguṇādipradatvam
yathā pañcame 
yasyāsti bhaktir bhagavaty akiñcanā
sarvair guṇais tatra samāsate surāḥ 
harāv abhaktasya kuto mahadguṇā
manorathenāsati dhāvato bahiḥ  RBhrs 
sukhapradatvam
sukhaṃ vaiṣayikaṃ brāhmam aiśvaraṃ ceti tat tridhā  RBhrs 
yathā tantre
siddhayaḥ paramāścaryā bhuktir muktiś ca śāśvatī 
nityaṃ ca paramānando bhaved govindabhaktitaḥ  RBhrs 
yathā haribhaktisudhodaye ca
bhūyo 'pi yāce deveśa tvayi bhaktir dṛḍhāstu me 
yā mokṣāntacaturvarga phaladā sukhadā latā  RBhrs 
mokṣalaghutākṛt
manāg eva prarūḍhāyāṃ hṛdaye bhagavādratau 
puruṣārthās tu catvārās tṛṇāyante samantataḥ  RBhrs 
yathā śrīnāradapañcarātre
haribhaktimahādevyāḥ sarvā muktyādisiddhayaḥ 
bhuktyaś cādbhutās tasyāś ceṭikāvad anuvratāḥ  RBhrs  iti 
sudurlabhā
sādhanaughair anāsangair alabhyā sucirād api 
hariṇā cāśvadeyeti dvidhā sā syāt sudurlabhā  RBhrs 
tatra ādyā yathā tāntre
jñānataḥ sulabhā muktir bhuktir yajñādipuṇyataḥ 
seyaṃ sādhanasāhasrair haribhaktiḥ sudurlabhā  RBhrs 
dvitīyā yathā pañcamaskandhe 
rājan patir gurur alaṃ bhavatāṃ yadūnāṃ
daivaṃ priyaḥ kulapatiḥ kva ca kiṅkaro vaḥ 
astv evam aṅga bhajatāṃ bhagavān mukundo
muktiṃ dadāti karhicit sma na bhaktiyogam  RBhrs 
sāndrānandaviśeṣātmā
brahmānando bhaved eṣa cet parārddhaguṇīkṛtaḥ 
naiti bhaktisukhāmbhodheḥ paramāṇutulām api  RBhrs 
yathā haribhaktisudhodaye
tvatsākṣātkaraṇāhlādaviśuddhābdhisthitasya me 
sukhāni goṣpadāyante brāhmāṇy api jagadguro  RBhrs 
tathā bhāvārthadīpikāyāṃ  ca
tvatkathāmṛtapāthodhau viharanto mahāmudaḥ 
kurvanti kṛtinaḥ kecit caturvargaṃ tṛṇopamam  RBhrs 
śrīkṛṣṇākarṣiṇī
kṛtvā hariṃ premabhājaṃ priyavargasamanvitam 
bhaktir vaśīkarotīti śrīkṛṣṇākarṣiṇī matā  RBhrs 
yathā ekādaśe 
na sādhyati mām yogo na sāṅkhyaṃ dharma uddhava 
na svādhyāyas tapas tyāgo yathā bhaktir mamorjitā  RBhrs 
saptame  ca nāradoktau
yūyaṃ nṛloke bata bhūribhāgā
lokaṃ punānā munayo 'bhiyanti 
yeṣāṃ gṛhān āvasatīti sākṣād
guḍhaṃ paraṃ brahma manuṣyaliṅgam  RBhrs 
agrato vakṣyamāṇāyās tridhā bhakter anukramāt 
dviśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ padair etan māhātyaṃ parikīrtitam  RBhrs 
kiṃ ca
svalpāpi rucir eva syād bhaktitattvāvabodhikā 
yuktis tu kevalā naiva yad asyā apratiṣṭhatā  RBhrs 
tatra prācīnair apy uktam
yatnenāpādito 'py arthaḥ kuśalair anumātṛbhiḥ 
abhiyuktatarair anyair anyathaivopapādyate  RBhrs 
iti śrī śrī bhaktirasāmṛtasindhau
pūrvabhāge bhaktisāmānya laharī prathamā 
dvitīyā laharī
sādhanabhaktiḥ
sā bhaktiḥ sādhanaṃ bhāvaḥ premā ceti tridhoditā  RBhrs 
tatra sādhanabhaktiḥ 
kṛtisādhyā bhavet sādhyabhāvā sā sādhanābhidhā 
nityasiddhasya bhāvasya prākaṭyaṃ hṛdi sādhyatā  RBhrs 
sā bhaktiḥ saptamaskandhe bhaṅgyā devarṣiṇoditā  RBhrs 
yathā saptame 
tasmāt kenāpy upāyena manaḥ kṛṣṇe niveśayet  RBhrs  iti 
vaidhī rāgānugā ceti sā dvidhā sādhanābhidhā  RBhrs 
tatra vaidhī
yatra rāgānavāptatvāt pravṛttir upajāyate 
śāsanenaiva śāstrasya sā vaidhī bhaktir ucyate  RBhrs 
yatha dvitīye 
tasmād bhārata sarvātmā bhagavān īśvaro hariḥ 
śrotavyaḥ kīrtitavyaś ca smartavyaś cecchatābhayam  RBhrs 
pādme ca
smartavyaḥ satataṃ viṣṇur vismartavyo na jātucit 
sarve vidhiniṣedhāḥ syur etayor eva kiṅkarāḥ  RBhrs 
ity asau syād vidhir nityaḥ sarvavarṇāśramādiṣu 
nityatve 'py asya nirṇītam ekādaśyādivatphalam  RBhrs 
yathā ekādāśe 
tu vyaktam evoktam
mukha bāhūrupādebhyaḥ puruṣasyāśramaiḥ saha 
catvāro jajñire varṇā guṇair viprādayaḥ pṛthak  RBhrs 
ya eṣāṃ puruṣaṃ sākṣād ātmaprabhavam īśvaram 
na bhajanty avajānanti sthānād bhraṣṭāḥ patanty adhaḥ  RBhrs 
tat phalaṃ ca tatraiva 
evaṃ kriyāyogapathaiḥ pumān vaidikatāntrikaiḥ 
arcann ubhyataḥ siddhiṃ matto vindaty abhīpsitām  RBhrs 
pañcarātre ca
surarṣe vihitā śāstre harim uddiśya yā kriyā 
saiva bhaktir iti proktā tayā bhaktiḥ parā bhavet  RBhrs 
tatra adhikārī
yaḥ kenāpy atibhāgyena jātaśraddho 'sya sevane 
nātisakto na vairāgyabhāg asyām adhikāry asau  RBhrs 
yathaikādaśe 
yadṛcchayā matkathādau jātaśraddho 'stu yaḥ pumān 
na nirviṇṇo nātisakto bhaktiyogo 'sya siddhidaḥ  RBhrs 
uttamo madhyamaś ca syāt kaniṣṭhaś ceti sa tridhā  RBhrs 
tatra uttamaḥ
śāstre yuktau ca nipuṇaḥ sarvathā dṛḍhaniścayaḥ 
prauḍhaśraddho 'dhikārī yaḥ sa bhaktāv uttamo mataḥ  RBhrs 
tatra madhyamaḥ
yaḥ śāstrādiṣv anipuṇaḥ śraddhāvān sa tu madhyamaḥ  RBhrs 
tatra kaniṣṭhaḥ
yo bhavet komalaśraddhaḥ sa kaniṣṭho nigadyate  RBhrs 
tatra gītādiṣūktānāṃ caturṇām adhikāriṇām 
madhye yasmin bhagavatah kṛpā syāt tatpriyasya vā  RBhrs 
sa kṣīṇatattadbhāvaḥ syāc chuddhabhaktyadhikāravān 
yathebhaḥ śaunakādiś ca dhruvaḥ sa ca catuḥsanaḥ  RBhrs 
bhuktimuktispṛhā yāvat piśācī hṛdi vartate 
tāvad bhaktisukhasyātra katham abhyudayo bhavet  RBhrs 
tatrāpi ca viśeṣeṇa gatim aṇvīm anicchataḥ 
bhaktir hṛtamanaḥprāṇān premṇā tān kurute janān  RBhrs 
tathā ca tṛtīye 
tair darśanīyāvayavair udāra
vilāsahāsekṣitavāmasūktaiḥ 
hṛtātmano hṛtaprāṇāṃś ca bhaktir
anicchato me gatim aṇvīṃ prayuṅkte  RBhrs 
śrī kṛṣṇacaraṇāmbhojasevānirvṛtacetasām 
eṣāṃ mokṣāya bhaktānāṃ na kadācit spṛhā bhavet  RBhrs 
yathā tatraiva
śrīmaduddhavoktau 
ko nv īśa te pādasarojabhājāṃ
sudurlabho 'rtheṣu caturṣv apīha 
tathāpi nāhaṃ pravṛṇomi bhūman
bhavatpadāmbhojaniṣevaṇotsukaḥ  RBhrs 
tatraiva śrīkapiladevoktau 
naikātmatāṃ me spṛhayanti kecin
matpādasevābhiratā madīhāḥ 
ye 'nyonyato bhāgavatāḥ prasajya
sabhājayante mama pauruṣāṇi  RBhrs 
tatraiva 
sālokyasārṣṭisāmīpya sārūpyaikatvam apy uta 
dīyamānaṃ na gṛhṇanti vinā matsevanaṃ janāḥ  RBhrs 
caturthe śrīdhruvoktau 
yā nirvṛtis tanubhṛtāṃ tava pādapadma
dhyānād bhavajjanakathāśravaṇena vā syāt 
sā brahmaṇi svamahimany api nātha mā bhūt
kiṃ tv antakāsilulitāt patatāṃ vimānāt  RBhrs 
tatraiva śrīmadādirājoktau 
na kāmaye nātha tad apy ahaṃ kvacin
na yatra yuṣmaccaraṇāmbujāsavaḥ 
mahattamāntarhṛdayān mukhacyuto
vidhatsva karṇāyutam eṣa me varaḥ  RBhrs 
pañcame śrīśukoktau 
yo dustyajān kṣitisutasvajanārthadārān
prārthyāṃ śriyaṃ suravaraiḥ sadayāvalokām 
naicchan nṛpas taducitaṃ mahatāṃ madhudviṭ
sevānuraktamanasām abhavo 'pi phalguḥ  RBhrs 
ṣaṣṭhe śrīvṛtroktau 
na nākapṛṣṭhaṃ na ca pārameṣṭhyaṃ
na sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam 
na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vā
samañjasa tvā virahayya kāṅkṣe  RBhrs 
tatraiva śrīrudroktau 
nārāyaṇaparāḥ sarve na kutaścana bibhyati 
svargāpavarganarakeṣv api tulyārthadarśinaḥ  RBhrs 
tatraiva indroktau 
ārādhanaṃ bhagavata īhamānā nirāśiṣaḥ 
ye tu necchanty api paraṃ te svārthakuśalāḥ smṛtāḥ  RBhrs 
saptame prahlādoktau 
tuṣṭe ca tatra kim alabhyam ananta ādye
kiṃ tair guṇavyatikarād iha ye svasiddhāḥ 
dharmādayaḥ kim aguṇena ca kāṅkṣitena
sāraṃ juṣāṃ caraṇayor upagāyatāṃ naḥ  RBhrs 
tatraiva śakroktau 
pratyānītāḥ parama bhavatā trāyatā naḥ svabhāgā
daityākrāntaṃ hṛdayakamalaṃ tadgṛhaṃ pratyabodhi 
kālagrastaṃ kiyad idam aho nātha śuśrūṣatāṃ te
muktis teṣāṃ na hi bahumatā nārasiṃhāparaiḥ kim  RBhrs 
aṣṭame śrīgajendroktau 
ekāntino yasya na kañcanārthaṃ
vāñchanti ye vai bhagavatprapannāḥ 
atyadbhutaṃ taccaritaṃ sumaṅgalaṃ
gāyanta ānandasamudramagnāḥ  RBhrs 
navame śrīvaikuṇṭhanāthoktau 
matsevayā pratītaṃ te sālokyādicatuṣṭayam 
necchanti sevayā pūrṇāḥ kuto 'nyat kālaviplutam  RBhrs 
śrīdaśame nāgapatnīstutau 
na nākapṛṣṭhaṃ na ca sārvabhaumaṃ
na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na rasādhipatyam 
na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vā
vāñchanti yatpādarajaḥprapannāḥ  RBhrs 
tatraiva śrīvedastutau 
duravagamātmatattvanigamāya tavāttatanoś
caritamahāmṛtābdhiparivartapariśramaṇāḥ 
na parilaṣanti kecid apavargam apīśvara te
caraṇasarojahaṃsakulasaṅgavisṛṣṭagṛhāḥ  RBhrs 
ekādaśe śrībhagavaduktau 
na kiñcit sādhavo dhīrā bhaktā hy ekāntino mama 
vāñchanty api mayā dattaṃ kaivalyam apunarbhavam  RBhrs 
tathā 
na pārameṣṭhyaṃ na mahendradhiṣṇyaṃ
na sārvabhaumaṃ na rasādhipatyam 
na yogasiddhīr apunarbhavaṃ vā
mayy arpitātmecchati mad vinānyat  RBhrs 
dvādaśe śrīrudroktau 
naivecchaty āśiṣaḥ kvāpi brahmarṣir mokṣam apy uta 
bhaktiṃ parāṃ bhagavati labdhavān puruṣe 'vyaye  RBhrs 
padmapurāṇe ca kārttikamāhātmye dāmodarāṣṭake
varaṃ deva mokṣaṃ na mokṣāvadhiṃ vā
na cānyaṃ vṛṇe 'haṃ vareśād apīha 
idaṃ te vapur nātha gopālabālaṃ
sadā me manasy avirāstāṃ kim anyaiḥ  RBhrs 
kuverātmajau baddhamūrtyaiva yadvat
tvayā mocitau bhaktibaddhau kṛtau ca 
tathā premabhaktiṃ svakāṃ me prayaccha
na mokṣe graho me 'sti dāmodareha  RBhrs 
hayaśīrṣīyaśrīnārāyaṇavyūhastave ca
na dharma kāmam arthaṃ vā mokṣaṃ vā varadeśvara 
prārthaye tava pādābje dāsyam evābhikāmaye  RBhrs 
tatraiva
punaḥ punar varān ditsur viṣṇur muktiṃ na yācitaḥ 
bhaktir eva vṛtā yena prahlādaṃ taṃ namāmy ahaṃ  RBhrs 
yadṛcchayā labdham api viṣṇor dāśarathes tu yaḥ 
naicchan mokṣaṃ vinā dāsyaṃ tasmai hanumate namaḥ  RBhrs 
ata eva prasiddham śrīhanumadvākyam
bhavabandhacchide tasyai spṛhayāmi na muktaye 
bhavān prabhur ahaṃ dāsa iti yatra vilupyate  RBhrs 
śrīnārada pañcarātre ca jitantestotre
dharmārthakāmamokṣeṣu necchā mama kadācana 
tvatpādapañkajasyādho jīvitaṃ dīyataṃ mama  RBhrs 
mokṣasālokyasārūpyān prārthaye na dharādhara 
icchāmi hi mahābhāga kāruṇyaṃ tava suvrata  RBhrs 
ataeva śrībhāgavate ṣaṣṭhe 
muktānām api siddhānāṃ nārāyaṇaparāyaṇaḥ 
sudurlabhaḥ praśāntātmā koṭiṣv api mahāmune  RBhrs 
prathame ca śrīdharmarājamātuḥ stutau 
tathā paramahaṃsānāṃ munīnām amalātmanām 
bhaktiyogavidhānārthaṃ kathaṃ paśyema hi striyaḥ  RBhrs 
tatraiva śrīsūtoktau 
ātmārāmāś ca munayo nirgranthā apy urukrame 
kurvanty ahaitukīṃ bhaktim itthambhūtaguṇo hariḥ  RBhrs 
atra tyājyatayaivoktā muktiḥ pañcavidhāpi cet 
sālokyādis tathāpy atra bhaktyā nātivirudhyate  RBhrs 
sukhaiśvaryottarā seyaṃ premasevottarety api 
sālokyādir dvidhā tatra nādyā sevājuṣaṃ matā  RBhrs 
kintu premaikamādhuryajuṣa ekāntino harau 
naivāṅgīkurvate jātu muktiṃ pañcavidhām api  RBhrs 
tatrāpy ekāntināṃ śreṣthā govindahṛtamānasāḥ 
yeṣāṃ śrīśaprasādo 'pi mano hartuṃ na śaknuyāt  RBhrs 
siddhāntatas tv abhede 'pi śrīśakṛṣṇasvarūpayoḥ 
rasenotkṛṣyate kṛṣṇarūpam eṣā rasasthitiḥ  RBhrs 
śāstrataḥ śrūyate bhaktau nṛmātrasyādhikāritā 
sarvādhikāritāṃ māghasnānasya bruvatā yataḥ 
dṛṣtāntitā vaśiṣṭhena haribhaktir nṛpaṃ prati  RBhrs 
yathā pādme 
sarve 'dhikāriṇo hy atra haribhaktau yathā nṛpa  RBhrs 
kāśīkhaṇḍe ca tathā
antyajā api tadrāṣṭre śaṅkhacakrāṅkadhāriṇaḥ 
samprāpya vaiṣṇavīṃ dīkṣāṃ dīkṣitā iva sambabhuḥ  RBhrs 
api ca
ananuṣṭhānato doṣo bhaktyaṅgānāṃ prajāyate 
na karmaṇām akaraṇād eṣa bhaktyadhikāriṇām  RBhrs 
niṣiddhācārato daivāt prāyaścittaṃ tu nocitam

bhindann aṇḍakaṭāhabhittim abhito babhrāma vaṃśīdhvaniḥ  RBhrs 
 rūpamādhuryaṃ
yathā tṛtīye 
yan martyalīlaupayikaṃ svayoga
māyābalaṃ darśayatā gṛhītam 
vismāpanaṃ svasya ca saubhagarddheḥ
paraṃ padaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣaṇāṅgam  RBhrs 
śrīdaśame ca 
kā stry aṅga te kalapadāyatamūrcchitena
saṃmohitā'ryapadavīṃ na calet trilokyām 
trailokyasaubhagam idaṃ ca nirīkṣya rūpaṃ

aparikalitapūrvaḥ kaś camatkārakārī

guṇātmanas te 'pi guṇān vimātuṃ
hitāvatīrṇasya ka īśire 'sya 
kālena yair vā vimitāḥ sukalpair
bhūpāṃśavaḥ khe mihikā dyubhāsaḥ  RBhrs 
nityaguṇo vanamālī
yad api śikhāmaṇir aśeṣanetṝṇām 
bhaktāpekṣikam asya
trividhatvaṃ likhyate tad api  RBhrs 
hariḥ pūrṇatamaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇa iti tridhā 
śreṣṭhamadhyādibhiḥ śabdair nāṭye yaḥ paripaṭhyate  RBhrs 
prakāśitākhilaguṇaḥ smṛtaḥ pūrṇatamo budhaiḥ 
asarvavyañjakaḥ pūrṇataraḥ pūrṇo 'lpadarśakaḥ  RBhrs 
kṛṣṇasya pūrṇatamatā vyaktābhūd gokulāntare 
pūrṇatā pūrṇataratā dvārakāmathurādiṣu  RBhrs 
sa punaś caturvidhaḥ syād dhīrodāttaś ca dhīralalitaś ca 
dhīrapraśāntanāmā tathaiva dhīroddhataḥ kathitaḥ  RBhrs 
bahuvidhaguṇakriyāṇām āspadabhūtasya padmanābhasya 
tattallīlābhedād virudhyate na hi caturvidhāḥ  RBhrs 
tatra dhīrodāttaḥ
gambhīro vinayī kṣantā karuṇaḥ sudṛḍhavrataḥ 
akatthano gūḍhagarvo dhīrodāttaḥ susattvabhṛt  RBhrs 
yathā
vīraṃmanyamadaprahārihasitaṃ dhaureyam ārtoddhṛtau

prekṣya tvāṃ mama durvitarkyahṛdayaṃ dhīr gīś ca na spandate  RBhrs

tad eteṣu tadādhikyapratipādanahetave  RBhrs

tattadbhaktānusāreṇa tathā kṛṣṇe vilokyate  RBhrs 
dhīralalitaḥ
vidagdho navatāruṇyaḥ parihāsaviśāradaḥ 
niścinto dhīralalitaḥ syāt prāyaḥ preyasīvaśaḥ  RBhrs

dhīraśāntaḥ

dhīroddhataḥ
mātsaryavān ahaṅkārī māyāvī roṣaṇaś calaḥ 
vikatthanaś ca vidvadbhir dhīroddhata udāhṛtaḥ  RBhrs 
yathā
āḥ pāpin yavanendra dardura punar vyāghuṭya sadyas tvayā

dhīroddhatas tu vidvadbhir bhīmasenādir ucyate  RBhrs

yathā vā
ambhobhārabharapraṇamrajaladabhrāntiṃ vitanvann asau

re śrīdāmakuraṅgasaṅgarabhuvo bhaṅgaṃ tvam aṅgīkuru  RBhrs

harau niraṅkuśaiśvaryāt ko 'pi na syād asambhavaḥ  RBhrs 
tathā ca kaurme

guṇā viruddhā apy ete samāhāryāḥ samantataḥ  RBhrs 
mahāvārāhe ca

hānopādānarahitā naiva prakṛtijāḥ kvacit  RBhrs

sarve sarvaguṇaiḥ pūrṇāḥ sarvadoṣavivarjitāḥ  RBhrs

aṣṭādaśamahādoṣai rahitā bhagavattanuḥ

aṣṭādaśamahādoṣāḥ
yathā viṣṇuyāmale

itthaṃ sarvāvatārebhyas tato 'py atrāvatāriṇaḥ 
vrajendranandane suṣṭhu mādhuryabhara īritaḥ  RBhrs

govindam ādipuruṣaṃ tam ahaṃ bhajāmi  RBhrs

nīce dayādhike spardhā śauryotsāhau ca dakṣatā 
satyaṃ ca vyaktim āyāti yatra śobheti tāṃ viduḥ  RBhrs 
yathā
svargadhvaṃsaṃ vidhitsur vrajabhuvi kadanaṃ suṣṭhu vīkṣyātivṛṣṭyā

vilāsaḥ

yathā
mallaśreṇyām avinayavatīṃ mantharāṃ nyasya dṛṣṭiṃ

yathā

yathā
anyāyyaṃ na harāv iti vyapagatadvārārgalā dānavā

yathā
pratikule 'pi saśūle

tejaḥ

yathā
tejo budhair avajñāder asahiṣṇutvam ucyate  RBhrs 
yathā
ākruṣṭe prakaṭaṃ didaṇḍayiṣuṇā caṇḍena raṅgasthale

yathā

atha kṛṣṇabhaktāḥ
tadbhāvabhāvitasvāntāḥ kṛṣṇabhaktā itīritāḥ  RBhrs 
yo satyavākya ity ādyā hrīmān ity antimā guṇāḥ 
proktāḥ kṛṣṇe 'sya bhakteṣu te vijñeyā manīṣibhiḥ  RBhrs

tatra sādhakāḥ
utpannaratayaḥ samyaṅ nairvighnyam anupāgatāḥ 
kṛṣṇasākṣātkṛtau yogyāḥ sādhakāḥ parikīrtitāḥ  RBhrs 
yathaikādaśe 
īśvare tadadhīneṣu bāliśeṣu dviṣatsu ca

siktāpy aśrujalotkareṇa bhagavadvārtānadījanmanā

atha siddhāḥ
avijñātākhilakleśāḥ sadā kṛṣṇāśritakriyāḥ 
siddhāḥ syuḥ santatapremasaukhyāsvādaparāyaṇāḥ  RBhrs 
samprāptasiddhayaḥ siddhā nityasiddhāś ca te tridhā  RBhrs 
tatra samprāptasiddhayaḥ
sādhanaiḥ kṛpayā cāsya dvidhā samprāptasiddhayaḥ  RBhrs 
tatra sādhanasiddhāḥ
yathā tṛtīye 
yac ca vrajanty animiṣām ṛṣabhānuvṛttyā
dūre yamā hy upari naḥ spṛhaṇīyaśīlāḥ 
bhartur mithaḥ suyaśasaḥ kathanānurāga
vaiklavyabāṣpakalayā pulakīkṛtāṅgāḥ  RBhrs 
yathā vā
ye bhaktiprabhaviṣṇutākavalitakleśormayaḥ kurvate
dṛkpāte 'pi ghṛṇāṃ kṛtapraṇatiṣu prāyeṇa mokṣādiṣu

nirdhautāsyataṭān muhuḥ pulakino dhanyān namaskurmahe  RBhrs 
mārkaṇḍeyādayaḥ proktāḥ sādhanaiḥ prāptasiddhayaḥ  RBhrs 
atha kṛpāsiddhāḥ
yathā śrīdaśame 
nāsāṃ dvijātisaṃskāro na nivāso gurāv api 
na tapo nātmamīmāṃsā na śaucaṃ na kriyāḥ śubhāḥ  RBhrs 
athāpi hy uttamaḥśloke kṛṣṇe yogeśvareśvare

yathā vā
na kācid abhavad guror bhajanayantraṇe 'bhijñatā

gato 'si caritārthatāṃ paramahaṃsamṛgyaśriyā
mukundapadapadmayoḥ praṇayasīdhuno dhārayā  RBhrs 
kṛpāsiddhā yajñapatnīvairocaniśukādayaḥ  RBhrs 
atha nityasiddhāḥ
ātmakoṭiguṇaṃ kṛṣṇe premāṇaṃ paramaṃ gatāḥ 
nityānandaguṇāḥ sarve nityasiddhā mukundavat  RBhrs 
yathā pādme śrībhagavatsatyabhāmādevīsaṃvāde

āgato 'haṃ gaṇāḥ sarve jātās te 'pi mayā saha  RBhrs

sarvadā matpriyā devi mattulyaguṇaśālinaḥ  RBhrs 
tathā ca śrīdaśame 
aho bhāgyam aho bhāgyaṃ nandagopavrajaukasām 
yanmitraṃ paramānandaṃ pūrṇaṃ brahma sanātanam  RBhrs 
tatraiva 
dustyajaś cānurāgo 'smin sarveṣāṃ no vrajaukasām 
nanda te tanaye 'smāsu tasyāpy autpattikaḥ katham  RBhrs

eṣāṃ laukikavacceṣṭā līlā muraripor iva  RBhrs 
tathā hi pādmottarakhaṇḍe
yathā saumitribharatau yathā saṅkarṣaṇādayaḥ 
tathā tenaiva jāyante nijalokād yadṛcchayā  RBhrs 
punas tenaiva gacchanti tatpadaṃ śāśvataṃ param 
na karmabandhanaṃ janma vaiṣṇavānāṃ ca vidyate  RBhrs

sakhāyo guruvargāś ca preyasyaś ceti pañcadhā  RBhrs

vayaḥsaundaryarūpāṇi kāyikāmṛdutādayaḥ  RBhrs

eṣām ālambanatvaṃ ca tathoddīpanatāpi ca  RBhrs 
tatra vayaḥ
vayaḥ kaumārapaugaṇḍakaiśoram iti tat tridhā  RBhrs

āṣoḍaśāc ca kaiśoraṃ yauvanaṃ syāt tataḥ param  RBhrs 
aucityāt tatra kaumāraṃ vaktavyaṃ vatsale rase

varṇasyojjvalatā kāpi netrānte cāruṇacchaviḥ

tathā
harati śitimā ko 'py aṅgānāṃ mahendramaṇiśriyaṃ

yathā śrīdaśame 
barhāpīḍaṃ naṭavaravapuḥ karṇayoḥ karṇikāraṃ

atha madhyamam
ūrudvayasya bāhvoś ca kāpi śrīr urasas tathā 
mūrter mādhurimādyaṃ ca kaiśore sati madhyame  RBhrs 
yathā
spṛhayati kariśuṇḍādaṇḍanāyoruyugmaṃ
garuḍamaṇikavāṭīsakhyam icchaty uraś ca 
bhujayugam api dhitsaty argalāvarganindām
abhinavataruṇimnaḥ prakrame keśavasya  RBhrs 
mukhaṃ smitavilāsāḍhyaṃ vibhramottarale dṛśau 
trijaganmohanaṃ gītam ity ādir iha mādhurī  RBhrs 
yathā
anaṅganayacāturīparicayottaraṅge dṛśau
mukhāmbujam udañcitasmitavilāsaramyādharam 
acañcalakulāṅganāvrataviḍambisaṅgītakaṃ
hares taruṇimāṅkure sphurati mādhurī kāpy abhūt  RBhrs 
vaidagdhīsāravistāraḥ kuñjakelimahotsavaḥ 
ārambho rāsalīlāder iha ceṣṭādisauṣṭhavam  RBhrs 
yathā
vyaktālaktapadaiḥ kvacit pariluṭhatpiñchāvataṃsaiḥ kvacit
talpair vicyutakāñcibhiḥ kvacid asau vyākīrṇakuñjotkarā 
prodyanmaṇḍalabandhatāṇḍavaghaṭālakṣmollasatsaikatā
govindasya vilāsavṛndam adhikaṃ vṛndāṭavī śaṃsati  RBhrs 
tanmohanatā yathā
vidūrān mārāgniṃ hṛdayaravikānte prakaṭayann
udasyan dharmenduṃ vidadhad abhito rāgapaṭalam 
kathaṃ hā nas trāṇaṃ sakhi mukulayan bodhakumudaṃ
tarasvī kṛṣṇābbhre madhurimabharārko 'bhyudayate  RBhrs 
atha śeṣam
pūrvato 'py adhikotkarṣaṃ bāḍham aṅgāni bibhrati 
trivalivyaktir ity ādyaṃ kaiśore carame sati  RBhrs 
yathā
marakatagirer gaṇḍagrāvaprabhāhararakṣasaṃ

tanutaraṇijāvīcicchāyāviḍambibalitrayaṃ
madanakadalīsādhiṣṭhoruṃ smarāmy asurāntakam  RBhrs 
tanmādhuryaṃ yathā
daśārdhaśaramādhurīdamanadakṣayāṅgaśriyā

sphurattaruṇimodgamaṃ taruṇi paśya pītāmbaram  RBhrs 
idam eva hareḥ prājñair navayauvanam ucyate  RBhrs 
atra gokuladevīnāṃ bhāvasarvasvaśālitā 
abhūtapūrvakandarpatantralīlotsavādayaḥ  RBhrs 
yathā
kāntābhiḥ kalahāyate kvacid ayaṃ kandarpalekhān kvacit
kīrair arpayati kvacid vitanute krīḍābhisārodyamam 
sakhyā bhedayati kvacit smarakalāṣāḍguṇyavān īhate
sandhiṃ kvāpy anuśāsti kuñjanṛpatiḥ śṛṅgārarājyottamam  RBhrs 
tanmohanatā yathā
karṇākarṇi sakhījanena vijane dūtīstutiprakriyā
patyur vañcanacāturī guṇanikā kuñjaprayāṇe niśi 
vādhiryaṃ guruvāci veṇuvirutāv utkarṇateti vratān
kaiśoreṇa tavādya kṛṣṇa guruṇā gaurīgaṇaḥ paṭhyate  RBhrs 
kuṇḍa iti kvacit
netuḥ svarūpam evoktaṃ kaiśoram iha yadyapi 
nānākṛtiprakaṭanāt tathāpy uddīpanaṃ matam  RBhrs 
bālye 'pi navatāruṇyaprākaṭyaṃ kvacit 
tan nātirasavāhitvān na rasajñair udāhṛtam  RBhrs 
atha saundaryam
bhavet saundaryam aṅgānāṃ sanniveśo yathocitam  RBhrs 
yathā
mukhaṃ te dīrghākṣaṃ marakatataṭīpīvaram uro
bhujadvandvaṃ stambhadyutisuvalitaṃ pārśvayugalam 
parikṣīṇo madhyaḥ prathimalaharīhāri jaghanaṃ
na kasyāḥ kaṃsāre harati hṛdayaṃ paṅkajadṛśaḥ  RBhrs 
atha rūpam
vibhūṣaṇaṃ vibhūṣyaṃ syād yena tad rūpam ucyate  RBhrs 
yathā

sā pratyuta svayam analpam alaṅkṛtāsīt  RBhrs 
atha mṛdutā
mṛdutā komalasyāpi saṃsparśāsahatocyate  RBhrs 
yathā
ahaha navāmbudakānter amuṣya sukumāratā kumārasya

ye nāyakaprakaraṇe vācikā mānasās tathā 
guṇāḥ proktānta evātra jñeyā uddīpanā budhaḥ  RBhrs 
ceṣṭā
ceṣṭā rāsādilīlāḥ syus tathā duṣṭavadhādayaḥ  RBhrs 
tatra rāso yathā
nṛtyadgopanitambinīkṛtaparīrambhasya rambhādibhir

duṣṭavadho

atha prasādhanam
kathitaṃ vasanākalpamaṇḍanādyaṃ prasādhanam  RBhrs 
tatra vasanam
navārkaraśmikāśmīraharitālādisannibham

tatra yugam
paridhānaṃ sasaṃvyānaṃ yugarūpam udīritam  RBhrs

tadupari navaraktaṃ vastram itthaṃ dadhānaḥ 
priyam iva kila varṇaṃ rāgayuktaṃ priyāyāḥ
praṇayatu mama netrābhīṣṭapūrtiṃ mukundaḥ  RBhrs 
catuṣkam
catuṣkaṃ kañcukoṣṇīṣatundabandhāntarīyakam  RBhrs 
yathā
smerāsyaḥ parihitapāṭalāmbaraśrīś

kaṃsārir vahati mahotsave mudaṃ naḥ  RBhrs 
bhūyiṣṭham

yathā
akhaṇḍitavikhaṇḍitaiḥ sitapiśaṅganīlāruṇaiḥ
paṭaiḥ kṛtayathocitaprakaṭasanniveśojjvalaḥ 
ayaṃ karabharāṭprabhaḥ pracuraraṅgaśṛṅgāritaḥ
karoti karabhoru me ghanarucir mudaṃ mādhavaḥ  RBhrs 
atha ākalpaḥ
keśabandhanam ālepo mālācitraviśeṣakaḥ

syāj jūṭaḥ kavarī cūḍā veṇī ca kacabandhanam 
pāṇḍuraḥ karburaḥ pīta ity ālepas tridhā mataḥ  RBhrs 
mālā tridhā vaijayantī ratnamālā vanasrajaḥ 
asyā vaikakṣakāpīḍaprālambādyā bhidā matāḥ  RBhrs 
makarīpatrabhaṅgāḍhyaṃ citraṃ pītasitāruṇam 
tathā viśeṣako 'pi syād anyad ūhyaṃ svayaṃ budhaiḥ  RBhrs 
yathā

yathā

tatra veṇuḥ

sarūpayor bhinnayor vā sandhiḥ syād bhāvayor yutiḥ  RBhrs

atha parārthā

tatra śāntoparasāḥ
brahmabhāvāt parabrahmaṇy advaitādhikyayogataḥ 
tathā bībhatsabhūmādeḥ śānto hy uparaso bhavet  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā
vijñānasuṣamādhaute samādhau yad udañcati 
sukhaṃ dṛṣṭe tad evādya purāṇapuruṣe tvayi  RBhrs 
dvitīyaṃ yathā
yatra yatra viṣaye mama dṛṣṭis
taṃ tam eva kalayāmi bhavantam 
yan nirañjana parāvarabījaṃ
tvāṃ vinā kim api nāparam asti  RBhrs 
atha prītoparasaḥ
kṛṣṇasyāgre 'tidhārṣṭyena tadbhakteṣv avahelayā 
svābhīṣṭadevatānyatra paramotkarṣavīkṣayā 
maryādātikramādyaiś ca prītoparasatā matā  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā
praṇayan vapur vivaśatāṃ satāṃ kulair
avadhīryamāṇanaṭano 'py anargalaḥ 
vikira prabho dṛśam ihety akuṇṭhavāk
caṭulo baṭuvyavṛṇutātmano ratim  RBhrs 
atha preyauparasaḥ
ekasminn eva sakhyena harimitrādyavajñayā 
yuddhabhūmādinā cāpi preyānuparaso bhavet  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā
suhṛd ity udito bhiyā cakampe
chalito narmagirā stutiṃ cakāra 
sa nṛpaḥ pariripsato bhujābhyāṃ
hariṇā daṇḍavad agrataḥ papāta  RBhrs 
atha vatsaloparasaḥ
sāmarthyādhikyābhijñānāl lālanādyaprayatnataḥ 
karuṇasyātirekādes turyāś coparaso bhavet  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā
mallānāṃ yadavadhi parvatodbhaṭānām
unmāthaṃ sapadi tavātmajād apaśyam 
nodvegaṃ tadavadhi yāmi jāmi tasmin
drāghiṣṭhām api samitiṃ prapadyamāne  RBhrs 
atha śṛṅgāroparasaḥ 
tatra sthāyivairūpyam
dvayor ekatarasyaiva ratir yā khalu dṛśyate 
yān ekatra tathaikasya sthāyinaḥ sā virūpatā 
vibhāvasyaiva vairūpyaṃ sthāyiny atropacaryate  RBhrs 
tatra ekatra ratir
yathā lalitamādhave
mandasmitaṃ prakṛtisiddham api vyudantaṃ
saṅgopitaś ca sahajo 'pi dṛśos taraṅgaḥ 
dhūmāyite dvijavadhūmadanārtivahnāv
ahnāya kāpi gaitri aṅkuritām ayāsīt  RBhrs 
atyantābhāva evātra rateḥ khalu vivakṣitaḥ 
etasyāḥ prāgabhāve tu śucir noparaso bhavet  RBhrs 
anekatra ratir yathā
gāndharvi kurvāṇam avekṣya līlām
agre dharaṇyāṃ sakhi kāmapālam 
ākarṇayantī ca mukundareṇuṃ
bhinnādya sādhvi smarato dvidhāsi  RBhrs 
kecit tu nāyakasyāpi sarvathā tulyarāgataḥ 
nāyikāsv apy anekāsu vadanty uparasaṃ śucim  RBhrs 
vibhāvavairūpyam
vaidagdhyaujjvalyaviraho vibhāvasya virūpatā 
latāpaśupulindīṣu vṛddhāsv api sa vartate  RBhrs 
tatra latā yathā
sakhi madhu kiratī niśamya vaṃśīṃ
madhumathanena kaṭākṣitātha mṛdvī 
mukulapulakitā latāvalīyaṃ
ratim iha pallavitāṃ hṛdi vyanakti  RBhrs 
paśur yathā
paśyādbhutās tuṅgamadaḥ kuraṅgīḥ
pataṅgakanyāpuline 'dya dhanyāḥ 
yāḥ keśavāṅge tadapāṅgapūtāḥ
sānaṅgaraṅgāṃ dṛśam arpayanti  RBhrs 
pulindī yathā
kālindīpuline paśya pulindī pulakācitā 
harer dṛkcāpalaṃ vīkṣya sahajaṃ yā vighūrṇate  RBhrs 
vṛddhā yathā
kajjalena kṛtakeśakālimā
bilvayugmaracitonnatastanī 
paśya gauri kiratī dṛgañcalaṃ
smerayaty aghaharaṃ jaraty asau  RBhrs 
sthāyino 'tra virūpatvam ekarāgatayāpi cet 
ghaṭetāsau vibhāvasya virūpatve 'py udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs 
śucitvaujjvalyavaidigdhyāt suveśatvāc ca kathyate 
śṛṅgārasya vibhāvatvam anyatrābhāsatā tataḥ  RBhrs 
atha anubhāvavairūpyam
samayānāṃ vyatikrāntir grāmyatvaṃ dhṛṣṭāpi ca 
vairūpyam anubhāvāder manīṣibhir udīritam  RBhrs 
tatra samayavyatikrāntiḥ
samayāḥ khaṇḍitādīnāṃ priye roṣoditādayaḥ 
puṃsaḥ smitādayaś cātra priyayā tāḍanādiṣu 
eteṣām anyathābhāvaḥ samayānāṃ vyatikramaḥ  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā 
kāntānakhāndhito 'py adya parihṛtya hare hriyam 
kailāsavāsinīṃ dāsīṃ kṛpādṛṣṭyā bhajasva mām  RBhrs 
atha grāmyatvam 
bālaśabdādyupanyāso virasoktiprapañcanam 
kaṭīkaṇḍūtir ity ādyaṃ grāmyatvaṃ kathitaṃ budhaiḥ  RBhrs 
tatra ādyaṃ yathā 
kiṃ naḥ phaṇikiśorīṇāṃ tvaṃ puṣkarasadāṃ sadā 
muralīdhvaninā nīvīṃ gopabāla vilumpasi  RBhrs 
atha dhṛṣṭatā
prakaṭaprārthanādiḥ syāt sambhogādes tu dhṛṣṭatā  RBhrs 
yathā
kānta kailāsakuñjo 'yaṃ ramyāhaṃ navayauvanā 
tvaṃ vidagdho 'si govinda kiṃ vā vācyam ataḥ param  RBhrs 
evam eva tu gauṇānāṃ hāsādīnām api svayam 
vijñeyoparasatvasya manīṣibhir udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs 
atha anurasāḥ
bhaktādibhir vibhāvādyaiḥ kṛṣṇasambandhavarjitaiḥ 
rasā hāsyādayaḥ sapta śāntaś cānurasā matāḥ  RBhrs 
tatra hāsyānurasaḥ
tāṇḍavaṃ vyadhita hanta kakkhaṭī
markaṭī bhrūkuṭībhis tathoddhuram 
yena vallavakadambakaṃ babhau
hāsaḍambarakarambitānanam  RBhrs 
atha adbhutānurasaḥ
bhāṇḍīrakakṣe bahudhā vitaṇḍāṃ
vedāntatantre śukamaṇḍalasya 
ākarṇayan nirnimiṣākṣipakṣmā
romāñcitāṅgaś ca surarṣir āsīt  RBhrs 
evam evātra vijñeyā vīrāder apy udāhṛtiḥ  RBhrs 
aṣṭāv amī taṭastheṣu prākaṭyaṃ yadi bibhrati 
kṛṣṇādibhir vibhāvādyair gatair anubhavādhvani  RBhrs 
atha aparasāḥ
kṛṣṇatatpratipakṣaś ced viṣayāśrayatāṃ gatāḥ 
hāsādīnāṃ tadā te 'tra prājñair aparasā matāḥ  RBhrs 
tatra hāsyāparasaḥ
palāyamānam udvīkṣya capalāyatalocanam 
kṛṣṇam ārāj jarāsandhaḥ solluṇṭham ahasīn muhuḥ  RBhrs 
evam anye 'pi vijñeyās te 'dbhutāparasādayaḥ 
uttamās tu rasābhāsāḥ kaiścid rasatayoditāḥ  RBhrs 
tathā hi
bhāvāḥ sarve tadābhāsā rasābhāsāś ca kecana 
amī proktarasābhijñaiḥ sarve 'pi rasanād rasāḥ  RBhrs 
bhāratādyāś catasras tu rasāvasthānasūcikāḥ 
vṛttayo nāṭyamātṛtvād uktā nāṭakalakṣaṇe  RBhrs 
granthasya gauravabhayād asyā bhaktirasaśriyaḥ 
samāhṛtiḥ samāsena mayā seyaṃ vinirmitā 
gopālarūpaśobhāṃ dadhad api raghunāthabhāvavisārī 
tuṣyatu sanātano 'sminn uttarabhāge rasāmṛtāmbhodheḥ 
iti śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhāv uttaravibhāge
rasābhāsalaharī navamī 
iti śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhau gauṇabhaktirasanirūpaṇo nāma caturtho vibhāgaḥ samāptaḥ 
rāmāṅgaśatrugaṇite śāke gokulam adhiṣṭhitenāyam 
bhaktirasāmṛtasindhur viṭaṅkitaḥ kṣudrarūpeṇa 
samāpto 'yaṃ śrīśrībhaktirasāmṛtasindhuḥ
